    1 $accept: Block EOF
             ;

    2 Block: '{' BlockStatements_opt '}'
           ;

    3 BlockStatements_opt: empty
    4                    | BlockStatements
                         ;

    5 BlockStatements: BlockStatement
    6                | BlockStatements BlockStatement
                     ;

    7 BlockStatement: LocalVariableDeclarationStatement
    8               | Statement
                    ;

    9 LocalVariableDeclarationStatement: LocalVariableDeclaration ';'
                                       ;

   10 LocalVariableDeclaration: VariableModifiers UnannType 
                                    VariableDeclaratorList
                              ;

   11 VariableModifiers: empty
   12                  | VariableModifier
   13                  | VariableModifiers VariableModifier
                       ;

   14 VariableModifier: /* empty */
                      ;

   15 UnannType: UnannPrimitiveType
   16          | UnannReferenceType
               ;

   17 UnannPrimitiveType: NumericType
   18                   | Boolean
                        ;

   19 NumericType: IntegralType
   20            | FloatingPointType
                 ;

   21 IntegralType: Int
   22             | Long
   23             | Char
   24             | Byte
   25             | Short
                  ;

   26 FloatingPointType: Float
   27                  | Double
                       ;

   28 UnannReferenceType: UnannClassOrInterfaceType
   29                   | UnannTypeVariable
   30                   | UnannArrayType
                        ;

   31 UnannClassOrInterfaceType: UnannClassType
   32                          | UnannInterfaceType
                               ;

   33 UnannClassType: /* empty */
                    ;

   34 UnannInterfaceType: UnannClassType
                        ;

   35 UnannTypeVariable: Identifier
                       ;

   36 UnannArrayType: /* empty */
                    ;

   37 VariableDeclaratorList: VariableDeclarator ',' VariableDeclarators
                            ;

   38 VariableDeclarators: empty
   39                    | VariableDeclarator
   40                    | VariableDeclarators ',' VariableDeclarator
                         ;

   41 VariableDeclarator: VariableDeclaratorId
   42                   | VariableDeclaratorId '=' VariableInitializer
                        ;

   43 VariableDeclaratorId: Identifier Dims_opt
   44                     | VariableInitializer
                          ;

   45 Dims_opt: /* empty */
              ;

   46 VariableInitializer: Expression
                         ;

   47 Statement: StatementWithoutTrailingSubstatement
   48          | LabeledStatement
   49          | IfThenStatement
   50          | IfThenElseStatement
   51          | WhileStatement
   52          | ForStatement
               ;

   53 StatementNoShortIf: StatementWithoutTrailingSubstatement
   54                   | LabeledStatementNoShortIf
   55                   | IfThenElseStatementNoShortIf
   56                   | WhileStatementNoShortIf
   57                   | ForStatementNoShortIf
                        ;

   58 StatementWithoutTrailingSubstatement: Block
   59                                     | EmptyStatement
   60                                     | ExpressionStatement
   61                                     | AssertStatement
   62                                     | SwitchStatement
   63                                     | DoStatement
   64                                     | BreakStatement
   65                                     | ContinueStatement
   66                                     | ReturnStatement
   67                                     | SynchronizedStatement
   68                                     | ThrowStatement
   69                                     | TryStatement
                                          ;

   70 EmptyStatement: ';'
                    ;

   71 LabeledStatement: Identifier ':' Statement
                      ;

   72 LabeledStatementNoShortIf: Identifier ':' StatementNoShortIf
                               ;

   73 ExpressionStatement: StatementExpression ';'
                         ;

   74 StatementExpression: Assignment
   75                    | PreIncrementExpression
   76                    | PreDecrementExpression
   77                    | PostIncrementExpression
   78                    | PostDecrementExpression
   79                    | MethodInvocation
   80                    | ClassInstanceCreationExpression
                         ;

   81 IfThenStatement: If '(' Expression ')' Statement
                     ;

   82 IfThenElseStatement: If '(' Expression ')' StatementNoShortIf Else 
                               Statement
                         ;

   83 IfThenElseStatementNoShortIf: If '(' Expression ')' 
                                        StatementNoShortIf Else 
                                        StatementNoShortIf
                                  ;

   84 AssertStatement: /* empty */
                     ;

   85 SwitchStatement: /* empty */
